        set hive.execution.engine=tez;

### <a name="dos--donts-between-cluster-versions"></a><span data-ttu-id="9803d-1513">DOS & zakazy między wersjami klastra</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9803d-1513">Dos & Don'ts between cluster versions</span></span>

### <a name="drivers"></a><span data-ttu-id="9803d-1664">Sterowniki</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9803d-1664">Drivers</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9803d-1665">Hello sterownik Java połączenia bazy danych (JDBC) dla programu SQL Server jest używana wewnętrznie przez usługi HDInsight i nie jest używane dla operacji zewnętrznych.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9803d-1665">hello Java Database Connectivity (JDBC) driver for SQL Server is used internally by HDInsight and is not used for external operations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9803d-1666">Jeśli chcesz tooconnect tooHDInsight przy użyciu otwarte połączenie bazy danych (ODBC), użyj hello sterownik Microsoft Hive ODBC.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9803d-1666">If you want tooconnect tooHDInsight by using Open Database Connectivity (ODBC), please use hello Microsoft Hive ODBC driver.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9803d-1667">Aby uzyskać więcej informacji, zobacz [tooHDInsight łączenie programu Excel z hello sterownik Microsoft Hive ODBC](hdinsight-connect-excel-hive-odbc-driver.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9803d-1667">For more information, see [Connect Excel tooHDInsight with hello Microsoft Hive ODBC Driver](hdinsight-connect-excel-hive-odbc-driver.md).</span></span>

### <a name="bug-fixes"></a><span data-ttu-id="9803d-1668">Poprawki błędów</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9803d-1668">Bug fixes</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9803d-1669">W tej wersji możemy odświeżeniu powitania po wersji usługi HDInsight kilka poprawki błędów:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9803d-1669">With this release, we have refreshed hello following HDInsight versions with several bug fixes:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="9803d-1670">HDInsight 2.1 (HDP 1.3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9803d-1670">HDInsight 2.1 (HDP 1.3)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="9803d-1671">HDInsight 3.0 (HDP 2.0)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9803d-1671">HDInsight 3.0 (HDP 2.0)</span></span>

## <a name="hortonworks-release-notes"></a><span data-ttu-id="9803d-1673">Informacje o wersji Hortonworks</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9803d-1673">Hortonworks release notes</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="9803d-1675">HDInsight w wersji 3.1 używa dystrybucji Hadoop, która jest oparta na powitania [platformie Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.7][hdp-2-1-7].</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9803d-1675">HDInsight version 3.1 uses a Hadoop distribution that is based on hello [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.7][hdp-2-1-7].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9803d-1676">Jest to klastra Hadoop domyślnego hello utworzenia przy użyciu portalu Azure powitania po 2014-11-7.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9803d-1676">This is hello default Hadoop cluster created when using hello Azure portal after 11/7/2014.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9803d-1677">Klastry HDInsight 3.1 utworzone przed 2014-11-7 znajdowały się na powitania [platformie Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.1][hdp-2-1-1]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9803d-1677">HDInsight 3.1 clusters created before 11/7/2014 were based on hello [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.1][hdp-2-1-1]</span></span>
